  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_9650df5f-9d54-4237-8646-4ac63bdb503c'
      });
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer4422381788763739017">With love for one another resting within their inseparable hearts, and a secret occupying their active, yet silent souls, seventeen-year-old Prince Nicu II and his sixteen-year-old sister Victoria, First Princess of Exubertis, must make a choice between their incestuous love affair, and the maintaining of stability within their royal family. Prince Nicu II and Princess Vic</span>
  <span id="freeText4422381788763739017" style="display:none">With love for one another resting within their inseparable hearts, and a secret occupying their active, yet silent souls, seventeen-year-old Prince Nicu II and his sixteen-year-old sister Victoria, First Princess of Exubertis, must make a choice between their incestuous love affair, and the maintaining of stability within their royal family. Prince Nicu II and Princess Victoria's immutable, romantic feelings for one another forces them to engage in extremely risky actions and fabricate various falsehoods. Throughout the play Nicu II and Victoria deceive everyone; including their parents King Nicu I and Queen Isabella. Nicu II is presumptuous in character, therefore, he maintains an excessive confidence within himself that he and his sister's romantic relationship can continue without being discovered, but Victoria fears that they cannot continue their affair emotionally unscathed. Despite Victoria's worries, she continues with the relationship as Nicu II emboldens her more and more.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4422381788763739017" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/76740720-robin-dixon?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/76740720-robin-dixon?shelf=plays">plays</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/76740720-robin-dixon?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/76740720-robin-dixon?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/76740720-robin-dixon?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/76740720-robin-dixon?shelf=theater">theater</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2265758791" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5511585673673418468">This play is very complex and detailed. I enjoyed it a lot. There is a lot of friction between the characters. It is high drama when it comes to content. Also, there is a lot of action within the story. One of the things I liked most about this book, was that the ending hit me out of nowhere. It comes on kind of suddenly and it is shocking. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/63922834-tracy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2025018164" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10168870627762291085">I have an appreciation for the overall plot of the play, as well as, the linguistic techniques that the playwright applies. The characters are unusual in their behavior, yet they maintain relatable and attractive attributes. I found the overall story to be emotionally moving and tragic. I would recommend this play to anyone who enjoys an alluring drama.<br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2278447247" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15130969661340424182">A modern tragedy, Nicu II, and Victoria's Incestuous Romance tell the tale of royal siblings having a love affair with one another. Prince Nicu II and Victoria hide their relationship from the rest of their family, as well as the public. Victoria is constantly pressured by their mother, Queen Isabella, who wants her to marry the prince of a neighboring kingdom known as Yorkton. Eventually, Isabella is told about the secret relationship of her two oldest children, by another of her children, Agri</span>
  <span id="freeText15130969661340424182" style="display:none">A modern tragedy, Nicu II, and Victoria's Incestuous Romance tell the tale of royal siblings having a love affair with one another. Prince Nicu II and Victoria hide their relationship from the rest of their family, as well as the public. Victoria is constantly pressured by their mother, Queen Isabella, who wants her to marry the prince of a neighboring kingdom known as Yorkton. Eventually, Isabella is told about the secret relationship of her two oldest children, by another of her children, Agripina. The results of the discovery are devastating to all involved in the end. </span>

    <a title="Morgan Nichols" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/83742808-morgan-nichols"><img alt="Morgan Nichols" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1530518136p2/83742808.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2442712098" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11931832877881195948">This is a good play. It features both drama and tragedy. A brother and sister in love and risking all to maintain it is the general theme. It's heavy on emotion and seriousness. It really has a very serious feel to it as all dramas should. Overall, this is an entertaining story. <br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>

<li class='cover' id='bookCover_264158'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/264158.The_Raven"><img alt="The Raven" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1347398489l/264158._SX98_.jpg" />

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('V1sZ4nFdHzARKfijivKFbZyrUYZ5sven5Hf7dtDyp8fHU9vUduHmrC9nZo31F+Brgs31mmeBJmFhTQ9BP0u58A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PhsjeUwYraYv4KwtZTew5HxsCD60ZCrsHVArqRZL9w+uE+FPS6RUOhGuMgMa0tXiYgqsIqpX+yqYat+e+fLpOA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

Early posthumously published collections-some of them featuring liberally “edited” versions of the poems-did not fully and accurately represent Dickinson’s bold experiments in prosody, her tragic vision, and the range of her intellectual and emotional explorations. Not until the 1955 publication of The Complete Poems of Emily Dickinson, a three-volume critical edition compiled by Thomas H. Johnson, were readers able for the first time to assess, understand, and appreciate the whole of Dickinson’s extraordinary poetic genius.\n\nThis book, a distillation of the three-volume Complete <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer15447023237479577950">Kenneth Jarrett Singleton is a thirty-two-year-old poet, playwright, and author. Prior to, "Exotic Neurotic," he had three of his books published. His first book was a science-fiction/horror novel called, "The Cadaver Factory." It was published in (2004) when Singleton was twenty years of age. His second novel, "The Donner Society," was published in (2005) the same year as his first play, "Angelic</span>
  <span id="freeText15447023237479577950" style="display:none">Kenneth Jarrett Singleton is a thirty-two-year-old poet, playwright, and author. Prior to, "Exotic Neurotic," he had three of his books published. His first book was a science-fiction/horror novel called, "The Cadaver Factory." It was published in (2004) when Singleton was twenty years of age. His second novel, "The Donner Society," was published in (2005) the same year as his first play, "Angelica and Francesca." He currently resides in the state of West Virginia. </span>
